25:T3c37,<entryFree id="n12714" key="دَفَعَهُ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">دَفَعَهُ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">دفع</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">دفعه</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">دفعة</orth>
                  </form>, (S, Msb, K,) aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Ba" lang="ar">دَفَعَ</orth>
                  </form>, (K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">دَفْعٌ</foreign> (Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">دَفَاعٌ</foreign> (TA) and <foreign lang="ar">مَدْفَعٌ</foreign>, (K,) [<hi rend="ital">He impelled it, pushed it, thrust it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">drove it;</hi> and particularly, <hi rend="ital">so as to remove it from its place; he propelled it; he repelled,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">repulsed, it; he pushed it, thrust it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">drove it, away,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">back;</hi>] <hi rend="ital">he put it away,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">removed it from its place,</hi> (Msb, TA,) <hi rend="ital">by,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">with, force,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">strength:</hi> (TA:) or <foreign lang="ar">دَفْعٌ</foreign> signifies the <hi rend="ital">putting away</hi> or <hi rend="ital">removing</hi> or <hi rend="ital">turning back</hi> a thing <hi rend="ital">before the coming</hi> or <hi rend="ital">arriving</hi> [of that thing]; like as <foreign lang="ar">رَفْعٌ</foreign> signifies the “ putting away or removing or turning back ” a thing “ after the coming or arriving ” thereof. (Kull p. 185.) Hence the saying in the Kur [ii. 252, and xxii. 41], <foreign lang="ar">وَلَوْ لَا دَفْعُ ٱللّٰهِ النَّاسَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And were it not for God's repelling men</hi>]; where some read   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n12714-1" target="دِفَاعُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n12722"/></foreign> [which means the same, as will be seen in the course of what follows, though bearing also another interpretation, likewise to be seen in what follows]. (TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">دَفَعْتُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الرَّجُلَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I impelled, pushed,</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">the man</hi>]. (S.) And   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n12714-2" target="دافعهُ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">دِفَاعٌ</foreign> [and <foreign lang="ar">مُدَافَعَةٌ</foreign>]; and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n12714-3" target="دفّعهُ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n12714"/></foreign>; (TA;) [both, app., accord. to the TA, signifying the same; but the latter more properly relates to several objects together, or signifies <hi rend="ital">he impelled it, pushed it,</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">much,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">vehemently,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">often;</hi> whereas] <foreign lang="ar">مُدَافَعَةٌ</foreign> (K, TA) and <foreign lang="ar">دِفَاعٌ</foreign> (TA) are [often exactly] <hi rend="ital">syn. with</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">دَفْعٌ</foreign>. (K, TA.) Thus, (TA,) you say, as meaning the same, <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n12714-4" target="دافع" n="4" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>عَنْهُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">دَفَعَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He repelled from him;</hi> whence another explanation of these two phrases, which see in what follows]. (S, TA.) And hence, <foreign lang="ar">دَفَعَ ٱللّٰهُ عَنْكَ المَكْرُوهَ</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">دَفْعٌ</foreign>, <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">May God repel,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">avert, from thee what is disliked,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">hated,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">evil</hi>]: (TA:) and <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n12714-5" target="دَافَعَ" n="5" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>ٱللّٰهُ عَنْكَ السُّوْءَ</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">دِفَاعٌ</foreign>, <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">May God repel,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">avert, from thee evil</hi>]. (S, TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">دَفَعْتُ عَنْهُ الأَذَى</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">I repelled,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">averted, from him what was hurtful,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">annoying;</hi> as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n12714-6" target="دَافَعْتُ" n="6" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>]. (Msb, K, TA.) Sb mentions, as a saying of the Arabs, <foreign lang="ar">اِدْفَعِ الشَّرَّ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">وَلَوْ إِصْبَعًا</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">Repel thou,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">avert thou, evil,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mischief, though but with a finger:</hi> the last word being in the accus. case by reason of the subaudition of the prep. <foreign lang="ar">ب</foreign>; the meaning being <foreign lang="ar">بِإِصْبَعٍ</foreign>]. (TA.) [See also an ex. voce <foreign lang="ar">دَفُوعٌ</foreign>.] When <foreign lang="ar">دَفْعٌ</foreign> is made trans. by means of <foreign lang="ar">عَنْ</foreign>, [and has a single objective complement, a second objective complement is understood, and in general] it has the meaning or the act of <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">Defending;</hi> as in the Kur [xxii. 39], <foreign lang="ar">إِنَّ ٱللّٰهَ يَدْفَعُ عَنْ ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">Verily God defendeth those who have believed;</hi> i. e. <hi rend="ital">repelleth from them</hi> aggression and the like]; (B;) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n12714-7" target="يُدَافِعُ" n="7" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, in the same, (K, TA,) accord. to another reading, signifies the same; (K, TA;) or this latter signifies <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">defendeth energetically, with the energy of him who contendeth for superiority in so doing.</hi> (Bd.) And <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n12714-8" target="دَافَعْتُ" n="8" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>عَنْهُ</foreign> signifies [also] <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">I pleaded,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">contended in arguments, in defence of him.</hi> (Msb.) [Exceptions to the statement cited above form the B will be found in what follows in this paragraph; and another exception, voce <foreign lang="ar">مُدَفَّعٌ</foreign>.]          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [In the exs. which follow, the verb is used in senses little differing, essentially, from those assigned to it in the first sentence of this art.]          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">دَفَعْتُ مِنَ الإِنَآءِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">دَفَْعَةً</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I poured forth from the vessel a single pouring</hi>]: the last word, which is with fet-h, is an inf. n. [of un.]. (Msb.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">دَفَعَتِ اللِّبَأَفِى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">ضَرْعِهَا قُبَيْلَ النِّتَاجِ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">She</hi> (a ewe, or goat, S, or a camel, S, K) <hi rend="ital">infused the first milk into her udder,</hi> i. e. <hi rend="ital">secreted it therein, a little before bringing forth</hi>]. (S, K.) And <foreign lang="ar">دَفَعَتِ اللَّبَنِ عَلَى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">رَأْسِ وَلَدِهَا لِكَثْرَتِهِ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">She</hi> (a ewe or goat, or a camel, TA) <hi rend="ital">secreted the milk in her udder when about to produce her young, by reason of its abundance</hi>]; for the milk becomes abundant in her udder only when she is about to bring forth: the inf. n. [app. the inf. n. of un.] is <foreign lang="ar">دَفْعَةٌ</foreign>. (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">دَفَعَتْ</foreign> alone, said of a ewe or goat, signifies <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical> <hi rend="ital">She secreted milk in her udder when about to produce the young;</hi> expl. by <foreign lang="ar">أَضْرَعَتْ عَلَى رَأْسِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الوَلَدِ</foreign> [which see in art. <foreign lang="ar">ضرع</foreign>]. (S, TA.)
